	html, body, div, span, object, iframe,
	h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, p, blockquote, pre,

	time, mark, audio, video, a {
		margin: 0;
		padding: 0;
		font-size: 100%;
		font: inherit;
		vertical-align: baseline;

	}
